                var len = this.length &gt;&gt;&gt; 0;

                var from = Number(arguments[1]) || 0;
                from = (from &lt; 0)
                        ? Math.ceil(from)
                        : Math.floor(from);
                if (from &lt; 0)
                    from += len;

                for (; from &lt; len; from++)
                {
                    if (from in this &amp;&amp;
                            this[from] === elt)
                        return from;
                }
                return -1;
            };
        }

   (function(){
            var D= new Date('2011-06-02T09:34:29+02:00');
            if(!D || +D!== 1307000069000){
                Date.fromISO= function(s){
                    var day, tz,
                            rx=/^(\d{4}\-\d\d\-\d\d([tT ][\d:\.]*)?)([zZ]|([+\-])(\d\d):(\d\d))?$/,
                            p= rx.exec(s) || [];
                    if(p[1]){
                        day= p[1].split(/\D/);
                        for(var i= 0, L= day.length; i&lt;L; i++){
                            day[i]= parseInt(day[i], 10) || 0;
                        };
                        day[1]-= 1;
                        day= new Date(Date.UTC.apply(Date, day));
                        if(!day.getDate()) return NaN;
                        if(p[5]){
                            tz= (parseInt(p[5], 10)*60);
                            if(p[6]) tz+= parseInt(p[6], 10);
                            if(p[4]== '+') tz*= -1;
                            if(tz) day.setUTCMinutes(day.getUTCMinutes()+ tz);
                        }
                        return day;
                    }
                    return NaN;
                }
            }
            else{
                Date.fromISO= function(s){
                    return new Date(s);
                }
            }
        })()
  </script>

    <script src="http://assets.staples-static.com/NDM2/sbdpas/20150701090436/js/jquery.tinycarousel.js" type="text/javascript">

    <input id="requestTypeAjax" type="hidden" value="false"/>
    <input id="eddiePageType" type="hidden" value="skuskuset"/>
    <script type="text/javascript">
     var dealBarCalled = false;
	var tinyBox;
	var summary_text = ["EXCLUSIVE OFFER","EXCLUSIVE OFFERS"];
	var dealBarSwitch = 'ON';
	function getDealBar(collectCallRequired,onLoad) {
		var parameters = {};
		parameters.storeId = propertyValues.DEF_STORE_ID;
		parameters.langId = propertyValues.DEF_LANG_ID;
		parameters.catalogId = propertyValues.DEF_CATALOG_ID;
		parameters.URL = $(location).attr('href');
		var pageName = "skuskuset";
		if("other" == pageName &amp;&amp; $('body').attr('id') == "skuskuset")
			pageName = "sku";
		
		parameters.pageType = pageName;
		var dealPromos = [];
		$("[id^='eddieDealBar_']").each(function(){
			dealPromos.push($(this).attr('id').split('_')[1]);
		});
		parameters.skuList = dealPromos.join(',');
		tinyBox = $('#divEddieSlider').data("plugin_tinycarousel");
		if(collectCallRequired)
			parameters.collectCallRequired = collectCallRequired;
		if(onLoad)
			parameters.onLoad = onLoad;
		if(!dealBarCalled || collectCallRequired || onLoad){
			$.ajax( {
				type : "post",
				url : propertyValues.POST_DOMAIN + "EddieCollectAjaxCmd",
				data : parameters,
				cache : false,
				success : function(response, status, xhr) {
				if('ON' == 'ON' &amp;&amp; $('#eddie-meerkat-wrap').length &gt; 0){
					try{
						var responseJSON = jQuery.parseJSON(response);
						var count = 0;
						if(collectCallRequired || onLoad){
							$('#treatmentGroupPerfectOfferDealBar').val(responseJSON.treatmentGroupPO);
							$('#treatmentGroupPerfectShippingDealBar').val(responseJSON.treatmentGroupPS);
						}
						$.each(responseJSON.skuCatMap,function(key,value){
							if($('#eddieDealBar_'+key).length &gt; 0){
								if(!onLoad){
									$('#eddieDealBar_'+key).html(responseJSON.catNameMap[value]).attr('href',responseJSON.catURLMap[value]);
								}
								if($('#promoPercentage_'+key).length &gt; 0){
									var promoPercent = $.trim($('#promoPercentage_'+key).text()).split('%')[0];
									$('#promoPercentage_'+key).text(parseFloat(promoPercent)+'%');
								}
							}else{
								if($('#eddieDealBar_').length == 1){
									$('#eddie_carousel').find('#eddieDealBar_').attr('id','eddieDealBar_'+key);
									$('#eddie-meerkat-wrap').show();
									$('.oo_feedback_float').css('bottom', '36px');
								}else{
									var tempCarousel = $('#eddie_carousel').clone();
									$(tempCarousel).find('[id^=eddieDealBar_]').attr('id','eddieDealBar_'+key);
									$('#eddie-offers-list').append(tempCarousel);
								}
								if(!onLoad){
									$('#eddieDealBar_'+key).html(responseJSON.catNameMap[value]).attr('href',responseJSON.catURLMap[value]);
								}
								var dealBarCurrSku = $('#eddieDealBar_'+key).parents('.pre-abandonment');
								$(dealBarCurrSku).find('[id^=promoPercentage_]').attr('id','promoPercentage_'+key).html(parseFloat(responseJSON.skuDiscMap[key])+'%');
								$(dealBarCurrSku).siblings('[id^=productCovPerfectOffer_]').attr('id','productCovPerfectOffer_'+key).val(responseJSON.skuPOCovMap[key]);
								$(dealBarCurrSku).siblings('[id^=productCovPerfectShipping_]').attr('id','productCovPerfectShipping_'+key).val(responseJSON.skuPSCovMap[key]);
							}
							++count;
						});
						if(onLoad &amp;&amp; 0 == count){
							$.each(responseJSON.skuDiscMap,function(key,value){
								if($('#eddieDealBar_'+key).length &gt; 0){
									if($('#promoPercentage_'+key).length &gt; 0){
										var promoPercent = $.trim($('#promoPercentage_'+key).text()).split('%')[0];
										$('#promoPercentage_'+key).text(promoPercent.replace(/\.0*$/,'')+'%');
									}
								}else{
									if($('#eddieDealBar_').length == 1){
										$('#eddie_carousel').find('#eddieDealBar_').attr('id','eddieDealBar_'+key);
										$('#eddie-meerkat-wrap').show();
										$('.oo_feedback_float').css('bottom', '36px');
									}else{
										var tempCarousel = $('#eddie_carousel').clone();
										$(tempCarousel).find('[id^=eddieDealBar_]').attr('id','eddieDealBar_'+key);
										$('#eddie-offers-list').append(tempCarousel);
									}
									$('#eddieDealBar_'+key).parents('.pre-abandonment').find('[id^=promoPercentage_]').attr('id','promoPercentage_'+key).html(value.replace(/\.0*$/,'')+'%');
									$('#eddieDealBar_'+key).parents('.pre-abandonment').siblings('[id^=productCovPerfectOffer_]').attr('id','productCovPerfectOffer_'+key).val(responseJSON.skuPOCovMap[key]);
									$('#eddieDealBar_'+key).parents('.pre-abandonment').siblings('[id^=productCovPerfectShipping_]').attr('id','productCovPerfectShipping_'+key).val(responseJSON.skuPSCovMap[key]);
								}
								++count;
							});
						}
						if(0 != count){
							dealBarCalled = onLoad ? false : true;
							var textForSummary = eval(count) &gt; 1 ? summary_text[1] : summary_text[0];
							$('#promoCount').text(count+" " + textForSummary);
							if(collectCallRequired){
								$('#eddie-promobar').animate({height:'136px'});
				            	$('.eddie_carousel-skin-eddie').slideDown();
				            	$('#eddie-maximize-link').hide();
				            	$('#eddie-minimize-link').show();
							}
							if(null != tinyBox){
								tinyBox.update();
								tinyBox.move(0);
							}
						}
						if(0 == eval(count)){
							$('#eddie-meerkat-wrap').hide();
						}
					}catch(e){
					}
				}
			},
			error : function(xhr, status, error) {
	
			}
			});
		}
	}
	STAPLES.Onload.addWindowEvent(function(){
    	  $("#divEddieSlider").tinycarousel({ infinite: false });
          $('.eddie-min-max-link').off('click').on('click',function(){
        	if ( $('#eddie-maximize-link').css("display") == 'none' ){
        		$('#eddie-promobar').animate({height:'31px'});
            	$('.eddie_carousel-skin-eddie').slideUp();
            	$('#eddie-maximize-link').show();
            	$('#eddie-minimize-link').hide();
            	$('.oo_feedback_float').animate({bottom:'36px'});
        	}else{
            	if(!dealBarCalled)
        			getDealBar(false,false);
        		$('#eddie-promobar').animate({height:'136px'});
            	$('.eddie_carousel-skin-eddie').slideDown();
            	$('#eddie-maximize-link').hide();
            	$('#eddie-minimize-link').show();
            	$('.oo_feedback_float').animate({bottom:'141px'});
        	}
        	
        });
          if(STAPLES != null &amp;&amp; STAPLES.EDDIE != null &amp;&amp; typeof STAPLES.EDDIE.updateDealBarData != 'undefined'){
        	  STAPLES.EDDIE.updateDealBarData();
          }else{
        	  getDealBar(false,true);
          }
    });
    </script>

     <div id="footerEmailSignup">
      <span>
       Deals! Get them now
      </span>
      <script type="text/javascript">
       /*
							Prevent context menu for all:
								oncontextmenu="return false;"
							Prevent ctrl-v:
								IE &amp; Webkit (Safari, Konqueror, etc.):
									onpaste="return false;"
								For Gecko (Firefox, Mozilla, Camino, etc.):
									onkeypress="return preventPaste(event);"
							*/
							function preventPaste(evt) {
								var isCtrl;
								var keyCode;
								var keyLetter;

								isCtrl = (evt.ctrlKey) ? true : false;
								keyCode = evt.charCode;
								keyLetter = String.fromCharCode(keyCode).toLowerCase();

								if(isCtrl &amp;&amp; keyLetter == "v") { evt.preventDefault(); }
							}
      </script>
     </div>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $('#custSvcList').html('&lt;a title="Customer Service" class="footerSlideLink"&gt;Customer Service&lt;/a&gt;').append($('.helpContent').html());
	$('#corpCustList').html('&lt;a title="Corporate Customers" class="footerSlideLink"&gt;Corporate Customers&lt;/a&gt;').append($('.corpCustomersContent').html());
	$('#corpInfoList').html('&lt;a title="Corporate Information" class="footerSlideLink"&gt;Corporate Info&lt;/a&gt;').append($('.corpInfoContent').html());
	if(jQuery('#custSvcHelp').find('#cstmrsrvc_stfdbck').length){//check if this element is on page
	 // Changes done for passing Session Id as an URL parameter to ForeSee - Site Monitoring and Tools changes. Logic changed to avoid Caching.
	 //DR-Stage changes: Added 'dcCookiePart' in Foresee URL to determine active datacenter
		var jSessionIdFlag = false;
		var jSessionId = STAPLES.Cookies.getCookie("JSESSIONID");
		var dcCookiePart = '&amp;StaplesDC=NDM2';
		if(jSessionId){
			if (jSessionId.indexOf(":") != -1 ) {
				jSessionIdFlag = true;
				var jSessionIdSplit = jSessionId.split(":");
				var urlWithJSessionId = jQuery('#custSvcHelp').find('#cstmrsrvc_stfdbck').attr('href') + '&amp;cpp[TLSessionID]='+jSessionIdSplit[0];
				var newUrlWithSessionId = 'javascript:STAPLES.Main.popUp("'+urlWithJSessionId+dcCookiePart+'", "", 1)';
				jQuery('#custSvcHelp').find('#cstmrsrvc_stfdbck').attr("href", newUrlWithSessionId);
			} 
		}	
		if(!jSessionIdFlag){ //Executes if JSession ID is not available or ":" is not in JSessionID cookie
			var actualUrl = 'javascript:STAPLES.Main.popUp("'+jQuery('#custSvcHelp').find('#cstmrsrvc_stfdbck').attr('href')+dcCookiePart+'", "", 1)';
			jQuery('#custSvcHelp').find('#cstmrsrvc_stfdbck').attr("href", actualUrl);
		}
	}
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function(){
		if (Modernizr.touch) {  
		  	//alert("It's a touch screen device.");
			touchFunctionality();
		}else if(('ontouchstart' in window) || !!(window.navigator.msMaxTouchPoints)){
			//This is for devices which does not support Modernizr		
			touchFunctionality();		
		}else{
			// This is for non-touch devices
		}
});

function touchFunctionality(){
		  	// Removal of header hover functionality
			$("#liwmsg").addClass("liwmsgMob").removeClass("liwmsgClass");
			$("#dealDropDown").addClass("dealDropDownMob").removeClass("dealDropDownClass");
			$(".navSelect").addClass("toolsHelpMob").removeClass("toolsHelp");
			// Removal of footer hover functionality
			$(".uxFooterMenu ul li.rollupItems").each(function(){
			    $(this).addClass("rollupItemsTouch").removeClass("rollupItems");
			});		
			
			
			$("#liwmsg,.navSelect,#dealDropDown,.uxFooterMenu ul li.rollupItemsTouch").on('click',function(){
				//Close Primary navigation				
				$("#wrapPrimaryNav .wrapPrimarySubnav").removeClass("expanded");
				$("#wrapPrimaryNav").removeClass("expanded");
				$("#wrapPrimaryNav ul.primaryNav li a").removeClass("active");
				// code for header part starts
				if($(this).data("checktouch").toString()!=""){
					if($(this).data("checktouch").toString()=="accLog"){ 
						$("#liwmsg span#yourAcctImg").toggleClass("yourAcctImgDown");
						
						$("#dealDropDown").removeClass("dealDropDownMobActive");
						$("#dealDropDown a.headNavLink").removeClass("headNavLinkDown");
						$(".navSelect").removeClass("toolsHelpMobDown");
						$("#dealDropDown,.navSelect").find('ul:first').hide();
					}
					else if($(this).data("checktouch").toString()=="dealDrop"){
						$("#dealDropDown").toggleClass("dealDropDownMobActive");
						$("#dealDropDown a.headNavLink").toggleClass("headNavLinkDown");
						
						$("#liwmsg span#yourAcctImg").removeClass("yourAcctImgDown");
						$(".navSelect").removeClass("toolsHelpMobDown");
						$("#liwmsg,.navSelect").find('ul:first').hide();
					}
					else if($(this).data("checktouch").toString()=="toolsDrop"){
						$(".navSelect").toggleClass("toolsHelpMobDown");
						
						$("#liwmsg span#yourAcctImg").removeClass("yourAcctImgDown");
						$("#dealDropDown").removeClass("dealDropDownMobActive");
						$("#dealDropDown a.headNavLink").removeClass("headNavLinkDown");
						$("#liwmsg,#dealDropDown").find('ul:first').hide();
					}			
					
					// footer menu hover deactivation	
					$(".uxFooterMenu ul li.rollupItemsTouch").each(function(){
						otherID = $(this).attr("id");
						$("#"+otherID).removeClass("footerTouchActive");
						$("#"+otherID).find('ul:first').hide();
					});
					
					$(this).find('ul:first').toggle();
				
				}else{
					//code for footer section starts
					var curID = $(this).attr("id");
					var otherID = "";
					$(".uxFooterMenu ul li.rollupItemsTouch").each(function(){
						otherID = $(this).attr("id");
				    	if(otherID == curID){
				    		$("#"+curID).find('ul:first').toggle();
				    		$("#"+curID).toggleClass("footerTouchActive");
				    		//console.log("======== "+curID+" ======== "+otherID);
				    	}
				    	else{
				    		$("#"+otherID).removeClass("footerTouchActive");
							//$("#"+otherID).find('ul:first').hide();
							
							$("#liwmsg span#yourAcctImg").removeClass("yourAcctImgDown");
							$("#dealDropDown").removeClass("dealDropDownMobActive");
							$("#dealDropDown a.headNavLink").removeClass("headNavLinkDown");
							$(".navSelect").removeClass("toolsHelpMobDown");					
							$("#"+otherID+",#liwmsg,#dealDropDown,.navSelect").find('ul:first').hide();
				    	}
				    	
					});
					//code for footer section ends
				}
	   		});	
			// Close all menus after clicking on Primary navigation
			$("ul.primaryNav li").on('click',function(){
				$(".uxFooterMenu ul li.rollupItemsTouch").removeClass("footerTouchActive");
				$("#liwmsg span#yourAcctImg").removeClass("yourAcctImgDown");
				$("#dealDropDown").removeClass("dealDropDownMobActive");
				$("#dealDropDown a.headNavLink").removeClass("headNavLinkDown");
				$(".navSelect").removeClass("toolsHelpMobDown");
				$(".uxFooterMenu ul li.rollupItemsTouch,#liwmsg,#dealDropDown,.navSelect").find('ul:first').hide();
			});
}

function updateHeaderRewardsLinkForRegUser() {
	if(!STAPLES.Main.isguest('StaplesUser')) {
		var rewardsLink = $("#staplesRewardsDashboardLink").val();
		if($("li#mccnt_stplsrwrds") != null) {
			$("li#mccnt_stplsrwrds a").attr("href", rewardsLink);
		}
		else if($("li#mccnt_stplsrwrdsrg") != null) {
			$("li#mccnt_stplsrwrdsrg a").attr("href", rewardsLink);
		}
	}
}

updateHeaderRewardsLinkForRegUser();

		function loadjscssfile(filename, filetype){
	 		if (filetype=="js"){
	  			var fileref=document.createElement('script');
	  			fileref.setAttribute("type","text/javascript");
	  			fileref.setAttribute("src", filename);
			}
	 		else if (filetype=="css"){
	  			var fileref=document.createElement("link");
	  			fileref.setAttribute("rel", "stylesheet");
	  			fileref.setAttribute("type", "text/css");
	  			fileref.setAttribute("href", filename);
	 		}
	 		if (typeof fileref!="undefined")
  				document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(fileref);
	 	}

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function writereview() {
        if ($('#openYotpoForm').length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; $('#openYotpoForm').val() === 'yes') {
            if(STAPLES.SkuTabs.getInfoTabs().find('li a[data-ref^=revs]').length &gt; 0){
               STAPLES.SkuTabs.getInfoTabs().find('li a[data-ref^=revs]').trigger('click');
            }
            if($('#yotpoReinitialized').length &gt; 0  &amp;&amp; $('#yotpoReinitialized').val() == 'no'){              
              yotpo.initialized = false;
              yotpo.init();
              $('#yotpoReinitialized').val('yes');
            }
            var api = new Yotpo.API(yotpo);
            api.openForm("review",1000);
       } else if (!STAPLES.Main.isguest('StaplesUser')){
          if(STAPLES.SkuTabs.getInfoTabs().find('li a[data-ref^=revs]').length &gt; 0){
               STAPLES.SkuTabs.getInfoTabs().find('li a[data-ref^=revs]').trigger('click');
          }
          if($('#yotpoReinitialized').length &gt; 0  &amp;&amp; $('#yotpoReinitialized').val() == 'no'){            
              yotpo.initialized = false;
              yotpo.init();
              $('#yotpoReinitialized').val('yes');
          }
          var api = new Yotpo.API(yotpo);
          api.openForm("review",1000);

           STAPLES.Main.popOverlay('/office/supplies/reviewform?langId=-1&amp;storeId=10001&amp;pr_page_id=1389313&amp;pr_source=web&amp;pr_campaign_id=skupage',15);
       }
        
    }

}
